At a Glance

The procedure of putting queries.

Matters to be judged from different houses.

Combinations leading to success of object in view.

Gain or Loss?

Immediate gain of wealth.

Foreign travels.

Return of a person in exile.

Missing person: Will he return or not?

Attack of enemies:Victory and defeat in wars.

Illness: Will the patient be cured or not?

Time of recovery from illness.

Identity of thief: Recovery of stolen articles.

Marriage: When will it take place? Nature of the wife etc.

Birth of children: Will the child be a boy or a girl?

Disputes:Master-servant relations.

Queries regarding dreams and meals.

Answering queries held in the mind of the consultor

FIRST

Prasnavatara
рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╛рд╡рд░рддрд╛рд░рд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ

рдирддреНрдпреЛрджрд┐рдЧрд░ рд╕рдордирд▓ рднреИрд░рд╡рдорд░реНрджреНрдзрддрдореАрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдВ рдиреГрд╣рд░рд┐рдореН ред

рд╡рд░рд╛рд╣реЗрдгреИрдпрд╛ рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрддреЗ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдиреЗ рд╡реИрдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрд╛рд░рдЪрд╛рдкред реерезрее

Having paid obeisance to Lord Narasimha who is fierce by his form and who is ever emitting fire from face, who is one without a second, and who is the over-lord of the entire universe, Sripati (Varahamihir) is writing this work Daivajna Vallabha dealing with the science of Horary Astrology.

NOTES: It is customary among Sanskrit writers to begin every work with an auspicious verse. The purpose of this prayer is to invoke the blessings of the lord : (1) for the completion of the work un-impeded by obstacles, (2) for the work to become popular in the world in future, (3) for observing the age old custom of great men and (4) for instructing the disciples that they too should do likewise.

It is generally belived that Sripati and Varahamihir are one and the same person. Sripati was the appellation granted to Varahamihir by king Vikramaditya in his honour for his correct prediction. This view is based on legends and as such may not get much credence today. We are however tempted to identify the one with the other on the basis that it was Varahamihir who authored Brihat Jataka in horoscopy, Pancha Siddhanta in the mathematical branch of astrology and Bribat Samhita in the Samhita branch and that it is the

sage again who authored the Prasna Vallabha in the horary astrology. Those having reservations in this respect are free to hold their views.

рджреАрдкреНрддрд╛рджреНрдпрдВ рджрд╢рднреЗрджрдВ рд╡реНрдпреЛрдордЪрд░рд╛рдгрд╛рдВ рдирд┐рд░реВрдкреНрдп рднрд╛рд╡рдлрд▓рдореН ред

рдкреГрд╖реНрдЯреЛ рдпрджреНрдпрддреНрдХрдердпрддрд┐ рд╢реБрднрд╛рд╢реБрднрдВ рддрддреНрддрджрдиреНрдпрдерд╛ рдиреЛрдХреНрддрдореН реереирее

The astrologer, who proclaims good and bad results after a deep consideration of the ten Avasthas (States) of planets and the results arising from the different houses, never goes [wrong1 Prasna Jnana, Sl. 2 (ii) Prasna Tantra I, Sls. 16-17").

NOTES: The Acharya will discuss the effects of planetary states at length in future chapters himself. The results of the houses have to be judged with reference to (1) the house itself; (2) the lord of the house; and (3) the significator of the house.

Vide-

рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рджреНрднрд╛рд╡рдкрддреЗрд╢реНрдЪ рдХрд╛рд░рдХрд╡рд╢рд╛рддреНрддрддреНрддрддреНрдлрд▓рдВ рдЪрд┐рдиреНрддрдпреЗрддреН ред

Same is the opinion of Acharya Bhattotpala and Nilakantha also. Such a conclusion arrived in this manner seldom goes wrong. In fact, all the authors are agreed on the point.

Almost all the classical writers have spoken of the avasthas or states of planets in their works and have held that these avasthas are also a source of strength for the planet to give the results. There is, however, some difference of opinion as regards the number as well as the nomenclature of avasthas. Nilakantha has stated ten avasthasnamely:Deeptha, 2. Dina, 3. Muditha, 4. Swastha, 5. Suptha, 6. Nipiditha, 7. Mushita, 8. Pariheena, 9. Swaveerya and 10. Adhiveerya.

Shri Mahadeva in Jataka Tatwa speaks of 5 avasthas in one classification which are: (1) Baala (child), 2. Kumar (boy), 3. Yuva (adult), 4. Vraddha (old) and 5. Mritaka (dead).

In another classification he details the avasthas as Shayana (lying down), 2. Upavesam (sitting), 3. Netrapani (hand on eyes), Prakasa (shining), 5. Gamana (going), 6. Aagamana (coming),

7. Sabha (in the assembly) 8.Gama, 9. Bhojana (eating) 10. Nrityalipsa (desiring to dance), 11. Kautuka (Curiosity) and 12. Nidra (sleeping). In another classification there are 7 avasthas. They are: 1. Deeptha, 2. Swastha, 3. Hasyayukta, 4. Shanta, 5. Shakta, 6. Lupta, 7. Peeditha.

In the Sanketa Nidhi there are 12 avasthas and 3 sub-avasthas of planets. The avasthas are 12 in number. namely: 1. Shayana, 2. Upaveshana, 3. Netrapani, 4. Prakasa 5. Gamana, 6. Agamana, 7. Aasthanee, 8. Aagama, 9. Bhuji, 10. Nrityalipsa, 11. Kautuka and 12 Nidra.

In Phala

Deepika we have eleven states. They are: 1. Pradeepta, (blazing) 2. Sukhita (happy), 3. Swastha (healthy). 4. Muditha (delighted), 5. Shanta (calm), 6. Shakta (competent), 7. Vikala (distressed), 8. Nipiditha (tortured or troubled), 9. Khala (Base), 10. Sudukhita (exceedingly unhappy) 11. Ati-bheeta (very much afraid)

рдореБрджрд┐рддреЛ рдорд┐рддреНрд░рдЧреГрд╣рд╕реНрдереЛ рд░рд┐рдкреБрдЧреЗрд╣рд╕реНрдпреЛ рднрд╡реЗрддреНрд╕реБрдкреНрддрдГ реерек рее

рдЕрдиреНрдпреИрд░реНрд╡рд┐рдЬрд┐рддреЛ рдпреБрджреНрдзреЗ рдирд┐рдкреАрдбрд┐рддреЛрд╜рд╕реНрддрдВрдЧрддреЛ рдореБрд╖рд┐рддрдГ ред

рдкрд░рд┐рд╣реАрдпрдорд╛рдирд╡реАрдпреЛрдВ рдиреАрдЪрд╛рднрд┐рдореБрдЦрдВ рдкреНрд░рд╕рд░реНрдкрд╢реНрдЪ рее рел рее

рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрдиреН рд╕реНрд╡реЛрдЪреНрдЪрд╛рднрд┐рдореБрдЦрдВ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд╡реАрд░реНрдпрдГ рд╕рдорд╛рдЦреНрдпрд╛рддрдГ ред

рд╢реБрднрд╡рд░реНрдЧрд╕реНрдердГ

рдЦреЛрдЯреЛрдзрд┐рдХрд╡реАрд░реНрдпреЛ рд╡рд┐рдкреБрд▓рд░рд╢реНрдорд┐рд╢реНрдЪ реерем рее

Planetary States : Diptha, (shining), Dina (miserable), Swastha (comfortable), Muditha (happy), Suptha (sleeping), Prapiditha (troubled), Mushita (robbed), Parihiyamanavirya (with power declining), Pravriddhavirya (with increased vigour), and Adhivirya (endowed with extreme power) are the ten planetary

state:

1. When the planet is placed in its exaltation sign is called

Diptha.

2. When it is in its debilitation sign, it is called Dina

3. In its own sign, the planet is termed Swastha.

4. In a friendly sign, it is called Muditha.

5. In an inimical sign, it is called Suptha.

6. When it is defeated in planetary war, it is termed Nipiditha.

7. While it is in heliocal setting, it is called Mushita.

8. While it is approaching its exaltation sign it is named Parihiyamanavirya.

9. While it is approaching its exaltation sign it is termed Pravriddhavirya.

10. The planet placed in the vargas of benefics after its rising, is called Adhikavirya.

Some of the terms are explained below:

*Exalted Planet-*The planets Sun to Saturn are exalted in the signs 1, 2, 10, 6, 4, 12 and 7 respectively. In these signs the respective planets are strong.

*Debilitated Planet -*The Sun to Saturn are in debilitation sign when they are respectively in 7, 8, 4, 12, 10, 6 & 1.

Neechabhimukh Planet- is one that is just to go into its debilitation sign e.g. Sun in Virgo, Moon in Libra.

Uchchabhimukh Planet- is one that is just to go into its exaltation sign e.g. Sun in Pisces, Moon in Aries.

рджреАрдкреНрддреЗ рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрд┐рджрдиреБрддреНрддрдорд╛ рдирд░рдкрддреЗрджреАрдиреЗ рдЪ рджреИрдиреНрдпрд╛рдЧрдордГ

рд╕реНрд╡рд╕реНрдереЗ рд╕реНрд╡реЗ рдордирд╕рд┐ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрдВ рдЪ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реАрдХреАрд░реНрддрд┐рд╕реМрдЦреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рдХрдореН ред

рдЖрдореЛрджреЛ рдореБрджрд┐рддреЗ рдпрдереЗрдкреНрд╕рд┐рддрдлрд▓рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд┐рдГ рдкреНрд░рд╕реБрдкреНрддреЗ рд╡рд┐рдХреНрддреНрдкреАрдбрд╛

рд╢рддреНрд░реБрдХреГрддрд╛ рдкреНрд░рдкреАрдард┐рддрддрдиреМ рдореЛрд╖рдВ рдЧрддреЗрд╜рд░реНрдердХреНрд╖рдпрдГ рее ренрее

рднрд╡рддрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд╡реАрд░реНрдпреЗ рдЧрдЬрддреБрд░рдЧрд╕реБрд╡рд░реНрдгрднреВрд▓рд╛рднрдГ ред

рддрджрджрдзрд┐рд╡реАрд░реНрдпрдпреБрдХреНрддреЗ рд╢рдХреНрддрд┐рддреНрд░рдпрд╕рдореНрдкрджрд╛рджрд┐рд╡рд╛рд╣реБрд▓реНрдпрдореН рее реорее

Results of Planetary states Diptha, etc : When a planet is in Diptha state full acquisition of the desired objects is to be foretold. If it be in the Dina state it indicates impending poverty.

If the planet be in the Swastha state, the object will be accomplished and there will be acquisition of wealth, fame andhappiness in addition. If it be in the Muditha state, there will be all-round happiness, and the accomplishement of desired objects.

If the planet be in the Prasuptha state, there will be danger and accidents etc. If it is in the Prapiditha state, there will be troubles through enemies. If it be in the Mushitha state, there will be loss of wealth. If the planet be in Pravriddhavirya state there will be acquisition of elephants, horses, gold and lands i.e. wealth. If it be in Adhivirya state, it bestows the three kinds of powers (рдЙрддреНрд╕рд╛рд╣, рдордиреНрддреНрд░, andрдкреНрд░рднреБ the powers of energy, good-counsel and majesty.) and extensive properties.

NOTES: The reader may study verses 22 to 24, Chapter I of Prasnatantra with benefit, wherein Nilakantha seems to follow Daivajnavallabha very closely.

Use of these principles in prediction is as follows: Suppose there is a query about acquisition of wealth. Suppose further that the lord of the ascendant and the lord of the eleventh house are both in the states Diptha, Swastha, Muditha or Adhivirya. Then it has to be interpreted that the object will be accomplished and that there will be acquisition of wealth. But if both these planets be in Mushita or Dina states, results will be quite opposite and unpleasant.

рдкреБрд╖реНрдкреИ рдлрд▓реИрдГ рдХрдирдХрд░рддреНрдирдпреБрддреИрдГрд╕реНрд╡рднреВрдореМ рдирдХреНрд╖рддреНрд░ рдЬрд╛рддрд┐ рд╕рд╣рд┐рдд

The duty of the querist: The querist should worship in his house, the planets and the rasi chakra (zodiacal diagram)] and the stars with flowers, fruits, gold and precious stones. He should be full of devotion towards God and the planets and should offer homage to deities and preceptors. Carrying flowers, gems, fruits and sacred vice he should go to the astrologer and pay respects to him and with great reverence, facing an auspicious direction (east, north etc.) he should put the query to him with a pure mind and that query should be put once only.

NOTES: Worship of rasi diagram is a customary ritual from ancient times and the same is considered to be an important part of the procedure of putting queries (рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдХрд░реНрдо). Its importance has been pointed out in almost all the works on Horary Astrology. For Example:

рд░рдореНрдпрддрд░реЗ рднреВрднрд╛рдЧреЗ рд╕рдореНрдкреВрдЬреНрдп рдЧреНрд░рд╣рдЧрдгрдВ рд╕рдирдХреНрд╖рддреНрд░рдореН ред

-Acharya Bhattotpala

рдкреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯрд╛ рд╕реБрднреВрдореМ рджреИрд╡рдЬреНрдЮрдВ рд╕рдХреГрддреНрдкреГрдЪреНрдЫреЗрддреНрдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЬрдирдореН рее

-Nilakantha

Prasna Tantra I рдкреНрд░рдХрд░рдг, Sls. 3 & 15

The reader may refer to Prasnamarga, Adhyaya II for further details in this regard.

The second point to be noted is that the querist should have faith in the science of Astrology and the astrologer and should not put questions for fun or mockery as it will go vain and has been forbidden by the shastras. Also only a single question should be put ata time.

The most important point to be noted in respect of the querist is that he should have absolute faith both in the science of astrology

as well as the astrologer. To ensure faith in the two the procedure prescribed is apparently more than enough. Nobody would worship the horoscope unless he has faith in astrology. As regards the faith in astrologer the querist is required to offer flowers etc. to the astrologer when asking the questions. Offering flowers is a sort of surrendering oneself to the astrologer which is not possible unless the person has a regard for the astrologer.

As regards the number of questions to be asked at one particular time the general directive is that only one question should be asked at a particular time. Daivajna Neela Kantha has also said the same thing. This restriction has been imposed perhaps for the reason that the answers are based on the ascendant and other houses in relation to it. One rasi remains on the horizon for abont two hours. Unless smaller divisions of a rasi by way of the cusp of the ascendant are studied it is not possible to answer many questions. If somehow more than one question at a time spring up in the mind of the querist there is a system prescribed for that also. First question should be replied to on the basis of the ascendant and the following questions, if any, should be replied to on the basis of the position of Moon, Sun and Jupiter etc. Some astrologers ask for a number either between 1 and 108 or 1 and 249 (both inclusive in each case). The sanctity of numbers 1 to 108 is that each rasi has nine padas of constellations. In other words the reply is based on the position of the cusps in the various padas of Constellations: One pada of the constellation will take less than 15 minutes to pass. The division of the Zodiac in 249 divisions appears to be a better practice because here we get very small Units and the Cusp would take about 4 minutes to change its position. The later procedure is generally known as Krishnamurti Padhdhati. The basis in each case is the smaller sub divisions of the Zodiac.

рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╛рдХреНрд╖рд░реИрд░реБрджрдпрд╣реЗрддреБрднрд┐рд░реБрд▓реНрд▓рд╕рджрд┐рдн-

рд░реНрдмрд╛рд╣реНрдпрд╕реНрдерд┐рддреИрд╢реНрдЪ рд╢рдХреБрдиреИрд░рдзрд┐рдЧрдореНрдп рд╕рдореНрдпрдХреН ред

рдкреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯреБрдГ рд╢реБрднрдВ рдЪ рдпрджрд┐ рд╡рд╛рдкреНрдпрд╢реБрднрдВ рдкреНрд░рдпрддреНрдирд╛рддреНрддрддреНрдХрд╛рд▓рдЬрдВ

рддрджрд┐рд╣ рджреИрд╡рд╡рд┐рджрд╛рдЬреНрдпрднрд┐рдзреЗрдпрдореН реерезрезрее

The astrologer should understand the good and bad results by considering carefully the syllables of the query as also the omens obtaining around and then proclaim the prediction for that time.2

рдлрд▓ рднрд░рдХреБрд╕реБрдорд╛рднрд┐рд░рд╛рдорднреВрдореАрд░реБрд╣рднреБрд╡рд┐ рдЧреЛрдордпрдкреБрд╖реНрдкрддреЛрдпрд╡рддреНрдпрд╛рдореН ред

рдЪрд░рдгрд╛рд╕реБрдЦрдХреГрддрд┐ рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрддрд╛рдВ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рджрднрд┐рдорддрд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрд┐рд░рд╕рдВрд╢рдпреЗрди рдкреБрдВрд╕рд╛рдореН рее резреи рее

If the query is put in a place charming trees laden with flowers, which, is rendered pure by cow-dung, flowers and water and a place pleasing to the eyes, surely men will accomplish their desired objects without any doubt.

рджреГрдХрдЪреЗрддрд╕реЛрдГ рд╕реБрдЦрдХрд░реА рдпрджрд┐ рднреВрдорд┐рд░рд╕реНрддрд┐

рдорд╛рдВрдЧрд▓реНрдпрд╡рд╕реНрддреБрд╡рд┐рд╖рдпреЗ рд╢реБрдн рджрд░реНрд╢рдиреЗ рдЪреЗрддреН ред

рдкреНрд░рдЪреНрдЫрд╛рд╡рд┐рдзреМ рд╢реБрднрдиреБрдкрд╕реНрдерд┐рддрдорд╛рджрд░реЗрдг рддрддреНрд░рд╛рдкрд┐

рд╡рд╛рдЪреНрдпрдорд┐рддрд┐ рд╡рдХреНрддрд┐ рднрдпреЛрдордгрд┐рддреНрдердГрее резрей рее

If the place is pleasing to the eyes and the mind, if there be sight of auspicious objects at the time of the query, good results in response to the query are bound to happen in near future thus say the acharyas Maya and Maniththa.

NOTES: Varahamihir has clearly stated in his Brihat Samhita that rsults of the query are influenced by the nature of the place where the query has been put.

“рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдВ…….рдЪрд┐рддрдВ рддреБрд╖реИрд╢реНрд╢реБрд╖реНрдХрддреГрдгреИрд░реНрдирд╢реЛрднрдирдореНрее”

Prasnasindhu, Muhurta Chintamani, Prasna Marga and other works have also stated that sight of auspicious objects during a query will definitely produce good results.

In the slokas 11 to 13 the sage has provided guide lines for the astrologer to start with the question. The first thing is that he should consider carefully the syllables of the questions which in themselves convey the results of the question to the astrologer. Daivajna Rama Dayalu in Sanketa VIII Sloka 16 has given the list of syllables owned

1.Prasna Jnana Sis 3-4. 2 Prasana marga..3 Cf. Prasna Jnana, SI. 5.

by various planets. They are a good guide to the astrologer in identifying the planet that is troubling the most.

Some astrologers do the work through the offerings brought by the querist. If it is the white Barfi the indication is that Venus is the main cause of worry. In the offerings the astrologers see the colour etc. and identify the planet. The experience shows that in most cases the offering does indicate the trouble.

The other important aid is the omen. Omens are events that occur unexpectedly at a particular moment of time. Butterfly in a hot summer noon in a room can never be imagined but they have been sighted and result predicted.

The third important factor that has been underlined here is the place where the question is asked. If it is a beautiful garden where the question is asked the result shall be different from what it would have been had the question been asked in a place where cow dung is stored.

While all of them are important aids over-emphasis on them is not desirable. It is finally the horary chart that should be relied upon. About the omens particularly much cannot be said. All omens are not to be taken into account. If a seriously ill person suddenly starts moaning, the same should not be considered as an omen. Further according to the Prasna Marga the results of omens concern past, present and future. Reference may be made to sloka 9 chapter 3 of Prasna Marga Part I published by Ranjan Publications.

рд╢рдХреБрдирдлрд▓рд╛рдирд╛рдордкрд┐ рднреВрддрд╛рдирд╛рдЧрддрд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдирддреНрд╡рдореН

Hence in the first place we have to see whether the omen is about the present, past or future. Then the analysis should follow. Analysis is also not an easy job. The same event can be interpreted differently in different cases. A man comes to ask a question about the possibility of his wife joining him. As he asks the question the lady of the house reports to the astrologer that the rope used for drawing the water from the well has been broken and the vessel tied with the rope has fallen into the well. Normally it can be interpreted

to mean that there is no hope of the union now because the last string of love has broken down. In fact this was the interpretation of all the disciples of the Daivajna except one who said that the string that was keeping away the water of the vessel to unite with the water of the well has been broken and that the couple will be happily re-united. Actually this is what happened. The wife united with the husband very soon and thereafter remained with him happily. Correct interpretation of the omen is very difficult. What is therefore most important is the horary chart and its analysis should be given pride of place in predctions.

In short the astrologer should be alert enough to watch around him. The touching of a part of the body by the questioner, the syllables uttered by him, the number given by him, offerings brought by him, sight of auspicious objects, soothing place and omens etc. have a bearing on the question in the mind of the questioner. The position of Moon and / or lagna-lord in Ithesala also help to understand the question before it is spelt out.

рдЗрддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реАрд╡рд░рд╛рд╣рдорд┐рд╣рд┐рд░рд╡рд┐рд░рдЪрд┐рддрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рджреИрд╡рдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╛рд╡рддрд╛рд░рд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ рдкреНрд░рдердордГ

Thus ends the I Chapter Prasnavatara (Beginning of the Query) in the work Daivajnavallabha of Varabamihira

SECOND

Good and Bad Results

рд╢реБрднрд╛рд╢реБрднрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ

рдкреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯреБрдГ рд╢реБрднреИрдГ рдкрдВрдЪрднрд┐рд░рд┐рд╖реНрдЯрд▓рд╛рднреЛрд╜рдирд┐рд╖реНрдЯрдкреНрд░рджреИрдГ рдкрдВрдЪрднрд┐рд░рдкреНрдпрдирд┐рд╖реНрдЯрдореН ред

рддреБрд▓реНрдпреИрд░реНрдмрд▓рд╛рдмрд▓рд╡рд╢рд╛рддреНрдлрд▓рдореВрд╣рдиреАрдпрдВ рдЬреНрдЮреЗрдпрдВ рдЪрддреБрд░реНрднрд┐рд░рде рд╡рд╛рдкрд┐ рдлрд▓рдВ рдмрд▓рд╛рдЪреНрдп рее рез рее

The five auspicious omens produce the achievement of desired objects. And the five inauspicious omens lead to undesirable result. If both auspicious and inauspicious omens seen, the result has to be told by a judgement of the strength of the omens. Results can be proclaimed on the basis of the strength of even four or less number of omens.

NOTES: Omens have been classified into five kinds : 1. sight of objects (animate or inanimate), 2. their sound, 3. their movement, 4. action, 5. utpata (unusual phenomenon portending evil). These have been discussed in great detail by Varahamihir in his Brihat Samhita. If all the five are auspicious, objects of query will be accomplished. If all are bad, it will not be achieved. Also the result of a weak omen is not to be taken into account. Only strong omens become the deciding factor.

Omens are the occurences that take place at the beginning of any event. Every occurence is not an omen. It should be something different from the common happening at the particular time.

Omens have been given pride of place in almost all classical works of horary astrology. Sage Varahamihir in his Brihat Samhita

1. (i) Vide Brihat Samhita-Chapter 46, and 86 to 95.
(ii) Cf:рд╖рдЯреН рдкрдВрдЪрд╛рд╢рд┐рдХрд╛Chapter I, Sl. 3.
рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди,SIs. 8-9 and 13-14
рдЬрд╛рддрдХрдкрд╛рд░рд┐рдЬрд╛рдд, Chapter XI, SI. 1.

says that the omens indicate the good or bad results of the native’s Poorva Karmas or the past deeds that are about to fructify at the present moment.

рдЕрдиреНрдпрдЬрдиреНрдорд╛рдиреНрддрд░рдХреГрддрдВ рдХрд░реНрдо рдкреБрдВрд╕рд╛рдВ рд╢реБрднрд╛рд╢реБрднрдореН

рдпрддреНрддрд╕реНрдпрд╢рдХреБрдирдГ рдкрд╛рдХрдВ рдирд┐рд╡реЗрджрдпрддрд┐ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрддрд╛рдореН рее

Chapter 86 sloke 5.

In Prasna Marga the learned author has asked the astrologer to pay special attention to some things and out of those things the omens are one that have to be given special consideration.

It may be stated here that the omens are not more general indications but are quite a comprehensive aid to divination. They indicate the directions also. The only thing is that the astrologer should be able to understand and interpret their correct meaning relevant to the query at hand. For a detailed study about the omens the readers are advised to refer to Brihat Samhita where the sage has classified the omens, and has also said which of the omens should be attended to and which ignored.

рднрд╛рд╡рдГ рд╕реНрд╡реЗрд╢реЗрдиреЗрдХреНрд╖рд┐рддреЛ рд╡рд╛ рдпреБрддрдГ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреНрдкрд╛рдкрд╛рджрдиреНрдпреИрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдкрд┐ рддрд╕реНрдпрд╛рд╕реНрддрд┐ рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐рдГред

рд╕реМрдореНрдпрд╛ рдпрд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдиреНрддреНрдпрд╛рд╕реНрддрдЦрд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдореНрдмреБрдЧрд╛ рд╡рд╛ рдкрд╛рдкреИрд░реЗрд╡рдВ рд╣рд╛рдирд┐рд╢рджреЗрд╢рдиреАрдпрд╛ рее реи рее

The house which is associated or aspected by its lord flourishes and yields its results fully. If the places 2, 4, 7, 10 and 12 counted from a house are occupied by benefics, the house flourishes. If the said places are occupied by malefics, it decays.

NOTES: There are some additional rules mentioned in other works which are noteworthy in this connection: (1) The house wherein a planet is in debilitation or inimical quarters decays. (2) If the lord of a house is placed in 6, 8 and 12th houses, the house decays. (3) If the lords of 6, 8 and 12th houses are placed in a malefic house, the house is destroyed. (4) The house having a large number Of vargas of malefics undergoes destruction. (5) The house where a planet is in exaltation, moolatrikona, friendly quarters or own sign

flourishes well. (6) The house having an abundancy of benefic vargas also flourishes well.

The houses 6, 8 and 12 are generally regarded as inauspicious and their lords as damaging the prospects of the houses occupied by them. As these houses are counted from the lagna they may be inauspicious or harmful in respect of the affairs of lagna like the health, accidents and death etc. They may be auspicious and helpful in the promotion of the affair of some other house or houses. The 8th house is 11th house counted from the 10th house. It shall therefore be helpful in the advancement of career etc.

The 5th house is

considered to be the most auspicious house. The same is not so if we are interested to know the gain or losses of the enemy because it is 11th to the 7th house, the house indicating the interest of the enemy. In fact the house should be reckoned from the house under judgement. This fact has been clearly stated by the Daivajna in slokas 17 and 18 of this very chapter.

Much has also been made of the dignities and other states of planets in respect of the planets occupying the house. It is a fact that neither all the planets signify the affairs of a particular house nor their exaltations etc. help to any appreciable extent their power of giving results. Fulfilment of the objects of the affairs of any house is a complicated affair. It does not depend upon any one of the planets. Sometimes the planet appears to be giving good results but ultimately it is realised that the same was tainted with equal amount of evil. Here is a case that shall prove the point.

The native has no child. Fifth house needs examination. The house is unoccupied. It has no evil aspect. Its lord Mars occupies kendra, not a bad position but he does not aspect his own house. Jupiter the karaka for childern occupies his own house. Being the

lord of kendra does not make him a functional malefic because he occupies the house. Despite this the native remains childless. Neither the lord of the house benefitted the native nore benefic Jupiter showered his grace. For reasons we have to go elsewhere. Here is another case. The native is unmarried. The lagna and lagnesh

are vargottam. Mercury the 11th lord is exalted. Jupiter is exalted in the 9th house. Venus the 7th lord as well as the kalatra karaka is also not very badly placed. Despite allthis the marriage was not given. It is true that there are reasons in the charts which explain ‘why’ of the matter. The point is that the dignities or other avastha’s do verylittle in giving the results.


рдкрд░реНрдпрд╛рдпрд╕рдВрдЬреНрдЮрд╛ рдЪреИрддреЗрд╖рд╛рдВ рдХрдереНрдпрддреЗ рдореБрдирд┐рд╕рдВрдорддрд╛ ред

рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╕рдВрдЬреНрдЮрд╛ рдЪ рддрд╕реНрдпреЛрдХреНрддрд╛ рддрд╕реНрдорд╛рддреНрдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╡рд┐рдЪрд╛рд░рдгрд╛ рее рей рее

The different synonyms of the names of the twelve houses as also the names acquired by them through their functions are being told according to the opinion of the ancient sages. From these the results of the querries have to be judged.

NOTES*:* Lagna, Prathama Bhava, Kalpa, Hora etc. are the paryayas or synonyms for the 1st house. Body, form, longevity etc. are the indications of the 1st house and these are called its functional names (рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╕рдВрдЬреНрдЮрд╛).

рдЖрд░реЛрдЧреНрдпрдкреВрдЬрд╛рдЧреБрдгрд╛рдХрд▓реНрдкрд╡реГрддреНрддрдорд╛рдпреБрд░реНрд╡рдпреЛрдЬрд╛рддрд┐рд░рджреЛрд╖ рд╕реМрдЦреНрдпрдореН ред

рдХреНрд▓реЗрд╢рд╛рдХреГрддреА рд▓рдХреНрд╖рдгрд░реВрдкрд╡рд░реНрдгрд╛рд╕реНрддрджреНрднрд╛рдЧрд┐рдиреЗрдпрд╕реНрдп рд╡рдзреВрд╕реНрддрдиреЛ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН рее рекрее

Health, honour, qualities, nature, conduct, age, state, caste, purity, happiness, misery, expression, form, colour nephew-All these are to be judged from the first house.

The first house has been termed as the house of the wife of the son of the sister because, the house of the sister is the 3rd, her progeny is 5th i.e. 7th and his wife is 7th from 7th i.e. first house.

рдорд╛рдгрд┐рдХреНрдпрд╕реБрдХреНрддрд╛рдлрд▓рд░рддреНрдирдзрд╛рддреБрджреНрд░рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдореНрдмрд░рд╕реНрд╡рд░реНрдгрд╣рдпрд╛рджрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрдореН
рд░реВрдкреНрдпрдВрд╕рдзрд╛рдиреНрдпрдХреНрд░рдпрд╡рд┐рдХреНрд░рдпрд╛рджрд┐рд╕рд╛рдзрд╛рд░рдгрддрджреНрднрд╡рддрд┐рджреНрд╡рд┐рддреАрдпреЗрее релрее

1. cf. (i) рднреБрд╡рдирджреАрдкрдХ, SI. 43.
(ii), рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирддрдиреНрддреНрд░,Sl. 33.
(iii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╢рд┐рд░реЛрдордгрд┐ I, Adhyaya, Sl. 2

Manikya (ruby), pearl, gem, metallic ores, articles, dress, gold, house, silver, grains, transactions, buying and selling - All these are to be judged from the 2nd house in general.

рд╕реНрдиреБрд╖рд╛рдиреБрдЬрдХреНрд╖реЗрдорд╕реБрдмреБрджреНрдзрд┐рд▓рд╛рднрднреГрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рджрд╛рд╕реАрднрдЯрдХрд░реНрдордХрд░реНрддреБрдГ ред

рднреНрд░рд╛рддреНрд░рд╛рджрд┐ рдЪрд┐рдиреНрддрд╛рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпрдВ рд╕рдордЧреНрд░рдВ рдкрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╛рдпрдореЗрддрддреН рдХрдерд┐рддрдВ рддреГрддреАрдпреЗ рее ремрее

Daughter-in-law, younger brother, welfare, intellect, gains, servants, servant maids, valorous actions and things relating to brotherтАФAll these are to be judged from the third house.

NOTES: Short travels, victory in debates, efforts and eating habits are also to be judged from this house.

Although normally the “wife of the son” is considered from the 11th house as the house is 7th (wife) of 5th (son). But if we adopt the dictum of “BHAVAT BHAVAM” we can take the house 5th to 5th i.e. 9th as the house of the son and his wife 7th from 9th i.e. the 3rd house.

рдЧреГрд╣рдВ рдирд┐рдзрд╛рдирдВ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд░рдкреНрд░рд╡реЗрд╢реЛ рдорд╣реМрд╖рдзрдХреНрд╖реЗрддреНрд░рд░рд╡рд▓рд╛рджрд┐рд╡рд╛рдЯреА ред

рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдЪреНрдпреБрддрд┐рд░реНрд▓рд╛рднрдЧреГрд╣рдкреНрд░рд╡реЗрд╢реМ рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐рд░реНрдЬрдирд┐рддреНрд░реА рдЬрдирдХрд╢реНрдЪ рддрджреНрд╡рддреН ред

рджреЗрд╢рд╛рджрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╛рдгреНрдпрдкрд┐ рд▓рд╛рднрдорд╕реНрдп рдкрд░реНрдпрд╛рдпрдореЗрддрддреНрдХрдердпрдиреНрддрд┐ рддреБрд░реНрдпреЗ рее рем рее

House, treasure, entry into caves and other holes, great medicines, cultivated lands, fields, orchards, friends, water, ceremonies in connection with ancestors, coming and going, village, happiness, demotions, loss of post, gains entry into a house, increase, parents, deeds relating to one’s native country and gains therefrom,тАУ all these are to be judged from the fourth house.

рдирд╛рдирд╛рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЧреЛ рд╡рд┐рдирдпрдкреНрд░рдмрдиреНрдзрдВрд╡рд┐рдиреЗрдпрд╡рд┐рджреНрдпрд╛рдирдпрдмреБрджреНрдзрд┐рдордВрддреНрд░рд╛рдГ ред

рд╕рдиреНрдзрд╛рдирдЧрд░реНрднрд╛рдЧрднрд╡рд╛рджрд┐рдХрдВ рдЪ рдкреНрд░рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рд╕реБрддрд╛рд░реНрдерд╕реНрдп рдЪ рдкрдВрдЪрдореЗ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН рее рем рее

Deeds of many kinds, humility, execution, planning, learning, Niti, intellect, hymns, chanting, compromise, pregnancy, children

1

.ef. (i) рднреБрд╡рдирджреАрдкрдХ, SI.45.

(ii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирддрдиреНрддреНрд░, SI. 35.

(iii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╢рд┐рд░реЛрдордгрд┐, Chapter ,I SI. 3.

intellect and happiness derived through children and wealth are matters to be judged from the 5th house.

рдЕрд╕реНрд╡рд╛рд╕реНрдереНрдпрджреМрд╕реНрдерд┐рддреНрдпрд╡рд┐рдкрдХреНрд╖рджрд╛рд╕рдХреНрд░реВрд░реЛрдЧреНрд░рдХрд░реНрдорд╛рдкрд░рдХреГрддреНрдпрд╢рдВрдХрд╛ ред

рдпреБрджреНрдзрд╛рджрд┐рддрдиреНрдорд╛рддреБрд▓рдорд╛рд╣рд┐рд╖рд╛рджреНрдпрдВ рд░реЛрдЧреЛрдкрд┐ рдЪрд┐рдиреНрддреНрдпреЛ рд░рд┐рдкреБрднрд╛рд╡рддреБрд▓реНрдпрдГ реерезреж рее

Ill health, bad state, enemies, servants, cruel deeds, heavy actions, witchcraft applied by enemies with an intention of killing enemies, doubts, wars, uncle, buffaloes, diseases, etc. are to be considered from the sixth house.

рд╡рд╕реНрддреБрдХреНрд░рдпрд╕реНрд╡рд╛рд╕реНрдереНрдпрд╡рдгрд┐рдЬреНрдпрд╡рд╛рджрдХрд╛рдореЛрджрдпреЛрджрд╛рд╕рдХрд▓рддреНрд░рдЪреМрд░реНрдпрдореН ред

рдирд┐рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐рд╕реНрд╡рд╕реНрддреНрд░реЗрдпрдЧрдорд╛рдЧрдгреНрдорд╛рджреНрдпрд╛рдВ рдХрд▓рддреНрд░рдкрд░реНрдпрд╛рдпрдорд┐рджрдВ рдирд┐рд░реБрдХреНрддрдореН реерезрезрее

Buying, health, trade, debates, lust, servants, wife, women’ thefts, returning from travel, sister’s son (nephew ), coming and going all these are denoted by the 7th house.

рдЖрдпреБрд░реНрд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзреЛ рдирд┐рдзрдирдВ рдЪ рд░рд╛рдЬреНрдпрдВ рднреЗрджреЛрд╜рде рд╡рд╛ рдмрдиреНрдзреБрдЬрдирд╕реНрдп рдЫрд┐рджреНрд░рдореН ред

рд╡реИрд╖рдореНрдп рджреБрд░реНрдЧрд╛рджрд┐рдХрд▓рддреНрд░рд╢рддреНрд░реБрд╡рдзреЛ рдирджреАрддрд╛рд░рдгрдорд╖реНрдЯрдорд░реНрдХреНрд╖реЗ реерезреи рее

Longevity and enmity, death, ruling powers, strife, quarrels, cleft, quarrels among relatives, hatred, places difficult to approach, fort, destruction of wife and enemies, crossing of rivers etc. are to be seen from the 8th house.

рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрджреАрдХреНрд╖рд╛рд╕реБрд░рдЧреЗрд╣рдпрд╛рддреНрд░рд╛ рдиреГрдкрд╛рднрд┐рд╖реЗрдХреЛ рдЧреБрд░реБрдзрд░реНрдордХреГрддреНрдпрдореН ред

рдЬрд▓рд╛рд╢рдпрд╢реНрдпрд╛рд▓рдХрджреЗрд╡рд░рд╛рджреАрдиреН рднреНрд░рд╛рддреБрд░реНрдЧреГрд╣рд┐рдгреНрдпреЛ рдирд╡рдорд╕реНрдп рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдГ реерезрей рее

Sacred study of books, intention in vedic temples, travels to holy places, love, coronation of kings, preceptor, meritorious deeds, reservoirs of water (wells, ponds, lakes etc.), brother-in-laws, brothers of husbands, and wives and governmental favour are matters to be seen from the ninth house.

рдЖрдХрд╛рд╢рд╡реГрддреНрддрд╛рдиреНрддрдЬрд▓рдкреНрд░рдкрд╛рддрдГ рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдВ рдкрд┐рддреБрдГ рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╕реБрдЦрд╛рджрд┐рдорд╛рдирдореН ред

1. Cf. (i) рднреБрд╡рдирджреАрдкрдХ, SI. 49.

(ii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╢рд┐рд░реЛрдордгрд┐, 1, SI. 5.

(ii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╢рд┐рд░реЛрдордгрд┐ Chapter, SI.8

Clues from the sky, rains, actions of one’s father and his place, respect, merit, country, power, authority, cows, fall from position, (displacements, demotions,) are judged from the tenth house.

NOTES: Clouds, lightning, storm, rains, hailstorms, capital, fame, travel to a foreign land, scandal etc. are also judged from this house

рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╕реНрдп рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐рдГ рдХреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐рдмреНрдзрд┐рд░реНрдЧрдЬрд╛рд╢реНрд╡рд╡рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рджрд┐рдХрдпрд╛рдирд╢рдпреНрдпрд╛рдГ ред

рд╕реНрд╡рд░реНрдгрд╛рдиреБрд╡рд┐рддреНрддрд╛рдк рд╣рддрд╛рджрд┐рдХрдиреНрдпрд╛рд▓рд╛рднреЛ рдЧрдЬрд╛рджреЗрдГ рд╢реНрд╡рд╢реБрд░рд╛рджреНрдпрдорд╛рдпреЗ рее резрел рее

Advancement of one’s actions, success in enterprises, gains from trade, elephants, houses, dress, transport, vehicles, bedding,loss of gold and wealth, gains of damsels and elephants, father-in-law are judged from the eleventh house.

NOTES: This house represents material prosperity of allkinds.

рддреНрдпрд╛рдЧрджрд┐рднреЛрдЧреЗрд╖реНрдЯрд┐ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд╛рд╣рджрд╛рди рдХреГрд╖реНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рдХрд░реНрдорд╡реНрдпрдпрд╕рдВрдХреНрд╖рддрд┐рд╢реНрдЪ \ред

рдкрд┐рддреГрд╡реНрдпрдорд╛рддреГрд╖реНрд╡рд╕реГрдорд╛рддреБрд▓рд╛рдиреАрдпреБрджреНрдзреЗрдХреНрд╖рдирдВ рдпреБрджреНрдзрдкрд░рд╛рдЬрдереЛрд╜рдиреНрддреНрдпреЗ реерезремрее

Renunciation, enjoyments, sacrifices, marriage, donation, cultivation, expenditure, injury, maternal uncle, mother’s sister, wife of maternal uncle wars, defeat in a war are matters to be seen from the 12th house.

It seems that the author is considering the maternal uncle from the 12th house on the assumption that the 10th house relates to the father and as such 3rd from it (12th) would be his younger brother. But in reality the house relating to father is the 9th and as such the 11th & not the 12th is the house of the younger brother of father.

рдпрджреНрдпрднрд╛рджреНрд╡реЗрд╖реБ рдпрджреНрд╡рд╕реНрддреБ рдХрдерд┐рддрдВ рдпрд╡рдирд╛рджрд┐рднрд┐рдГ ред

рддрддреНрдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╕рдВрдЬреНрдЮрдорд╛рдЦреНрдпрд╛рддрдВ рддрддрдГ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╡рд┐рдЪрд╛рд░рд╛рдгрд╛ рее резрен рее

The objects that are to be judged from the different houses as proclaimed by the great Acharyas, Yavana etc. become the functional names attributed to the house. From the corresponding house, the objects should be judged, in a query.

рдпрд╕реНрдп рднрд╛рд╡рд╕реНрдп рдпрджреНрд╡рд╕реНрддреБ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдорд╛рддреНрд░реЗ рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд╢рд┐рддрдореН ред

рддрддреНрдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рддреБ рддрд▓реНрд▓рдЧреНрдирдореЗрд╡ рд╡рд╛ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рд╡рджреНрднрд╡реЗрддреН рее резрео рее

While answering queries, whatever object is under consideration, the house representing the same should be treated as the ascendant and the results declared.

рдпрджреНрдпрджреНрднрд╛рд╡реЗрд╖реБ рдпрддреНрдХрд░реНрдо рддрд╕реНрдорд╛рд▓реНрд▓рдЧреНрдирд╡реНрдпрд╡рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд┐рдГ ред

рдЕрддреАрддрд╛рдирд╛рдЧрддреЗ рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпреЗ рддреНрд╡рддреАрддрд╛рдирд╛рдЧрддрд╛рджрдкрд┐ реерезрепрее

From the functions attributed to the different houses, the ascendant has to be determined as told above. Past has to be judged from the 12th house and future from the 2nd house.

рдореВрд░реНрджреНрдзреЛрджрдпреЗ рд╕реМрдореНрдпрд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирдЧреЗ рд╡рд╛ рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗрд╜рдкрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рд╕реМрдореНрдпрдпреБрддреЗ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН ред

рдЕрддреЛрд╜рдиреНрдпрдерд╛рддреНрд╡реЗ рддреБ рддрджрдиреНрдпрдерд╛рддреНрд╡рдВ рдорд┐рд╢реНрд░рдВ рд╡рд┐рдорд┐рд╢реНрд░реИрд░рдзрд┐рдХрдВ рдмрд▓рд╛рдвреНрдпреИ рее реиреж рее

Combinations for success of the object of the query: If the ascendant falls in a sirshodaya sign or in the sign of a benefic planet, the result of the query will be auspicious. Under opposite circumstances, results will be just the reverse. If the circumstances are mixed, results will be also found to be of mixed nature.

NOTES: (i) Gemini, Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Aquarius are Sirshodaya signs.

(ii) Aries, Taurus, Cancer, Sagittarius and Capricorn are the Prishthodaya signs.

(iii) Prithuyasas says that under mixed circumstances the object to the query will be accomplished with great difficulty.

рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░реЛрдкрдЧрд╛ рдирд╡рдордкрдВрдЪрдордЧрд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рд╕реМрдореНрдпрд╛рдГ

рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рд╖реНрдЯрд╡рд░реНрдЬреНрдпрдорд╢реБрднрд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд┐рд╖рдбрд╛рдпрд╕рдВрд╕реНрдерд╛рдГ ред

рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╛рд░реНрдерд╕рд╛рдзрдирдХрд░рд╛рдГ рдкрд░рд┐рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрддрд╛рдВ рд╕реНрдпреБрд░реЗрднрд┐

рд░реНрд╡рд┐рдкрд░реНрдпрдЧреБрдгреИрд╕реНрддреБ рд╡рд┐рдкрд░реНрдпрдпрдГ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН реереирезрее

All the desired objects are achieved if the benefics occupy the quadrants (1, 4, 7 & 10) and the thrikona houses (5 and 9) and at the same time malefics are situated in the house 3, 6 and 11 and they do not occupy the angular house (1, 4, 7 & 10) and the 8th house.

1. Judgement of Longevity by D.P.Saxen.

2. Cr. (i)рд╖рдЯреН рдпрдВрдЪрд╛рд╢рд┐рдХ-Chapter IV, Sloka I.

(ii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди Sloka 88

(iii)рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╡реИрд╖реНрдгрд╡-Chapter 1, Sloka 7.

рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рдзрд┐рдирд╛рдереЛ рдпрджрд┐ рд▓рдЧреНрдирдЧрдГ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреНрддрдиреНрдорд┐рддреНрд░рдореЗрддрд╕реНрдп рдЪ рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдЧрдВ рд╡рд╛ ред

рд╡реНрдпрдпрд╛рд╖реНрдЯрдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рдгреНрдпрдкрд╣рд╛рдп рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рд╢реНрдЪрд╛рдиреНрдпрддреНрд░ рдпрд╛рддрд╛рджрд┐ рддрдЪреНрдЫреБрднрдВ рдпрд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН реереиреи рее

If the lord of an angular house is placed in the ascendant or the friend of the lord of the ascendant be placed in an angular house and malefic planets do not occupy Kendras, 8th house and the 12th house (1, 4, 7, 10, 8 and 12), the result of the query will be auspicious.

NOTES: Bhattotpala says:

рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╛рдзрд┐рдкрддрд┐рдГ рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░реЗ рддрдиреНрдорд┐рддреНрд░рдВ рд╡рд╛ рд╡реНрдпрдпрд╛рд╖реНрдЯрдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░реЗрднреНрдпрдГ ред

рдЕрдиреНрдпрддреНрд░рдЧрддрд╛рдГ рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рдГ рддрддреНрд░рд╛рдкрд┐ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╡рджреЗрддреНрдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдиреЗрее рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЬреНрдЮрд╛реж рее

рдирд░рд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирдорд╛рднрдорд┐рд╡реАрдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрдВ рд╢реБрднреИрд░реБрджрдпрд╛рд╕реНрддрдмрдиреНрдзреБрджрд╢рдЧреИрдГ рд╢реБрднреИрд╕реНрддрдерд╛ ред

рддреНрд░рд┐рдХрд╛рд▓рд╛рднрд╖рд╖реНрдарднрдЧрддреИрд╕реНрдерд╛рд╜рд╢реБрднреИрдГ рд╢реБрднрд▓рд╛рднрд╡рд┐рддреНрддрд╡рд┐рд╖рдпрд╛рдВрд╕реНрддрджрд╛ рд╡рджреЗрддреН реереирейрее

If the ascendant falls in a human sign, and be aspected by benefic planets or if benefics occupy 1st, 4th, 7th, and 10th houses, and malefics occupy 3rd, 6th and 11th houses, good results, gains and financial prosperity have to be foretold.

рддреЗрд╖реБрд╕реМрдореНрдпрд╕рд╣рд┐рддреЗрд╖реБ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╡рд┐рднрд╛рд╡реНрдпрдореН ред

рдкрд╛рдкрд╛ рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдпрднрдЧрддрд╛ рди рд╢реБрднрд╛ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдкрд╛рдкрдГ

рд╢рд╢рд┐ рди рд╢реБрднрджреЛ рджрд╢рдореЗ рд╢реБрднрд╢реНрдЪ реереирекрее

The signs Gemini, Virgo, Tula, Aquarius are termed human signs. If benefics are placed in these signs, results will be auspicious. Malefics in the 11th and 12th houses will not yield good results. Weak Moon in the ascendant is not good. But in the 10th house it is good.

NOTES : The Moon is weak from Dasami (10th) of the dark half (Krishna Paksha) to the Panchami (5th) of the bright half (Sukla Paksha). Other authors are of the opinion that Moon is weak from Ashtami (8th) of Krishna Paksha to Saptami (7th) of Sukla paksha.

рдЪрддреБрд╖реНрдкрджреЗ рд╡рд╛ рджреНрд╡рд┐рдкрджреЗ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдкрд╛рдкрдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╕реНрдереЗрди рддрджреАрдХреНрд╖рд┐рддреИрд╢реНрдЪ ред

рд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣реИрд╕реНрддреНрд╡реАрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдд рдПрд╡ рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐ рдиреГрд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рддреБ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╕рдорд╕реНрддрдореН рее реирелрее

If the ascendant falls in a biped or a quadruped sign and is aspected by a malefic planet troubles will arise. But if aspected by benefic planet good results will arise. If there is a human sign on the ascendant, all the results will be good.

NOTES: Biped signs-Gemini, Virgo, Tula, the first half of Sagittarius and Aquarius. Quadruped signs: Aries, Taurus, Leo, and the Latter half of Sagittarius.

рдЙрджрдпрддреБрд╣рд┐рдирджреАрдзрд┐рддреА рднрд╡реЗрддрд╛рдВ рдпрджрд┐ рдЪ рд╢реБрднреИрд░рдорд┐рд╡реАрдХреНрд╖рд┐рддреМ рддрджрд╛рдиреАрдореН ред

рд╢реБрднрдорд╢реБрднрдорддреЛрд╜рдиреНрдпрдереЗрддреНрдпрднреАрд╖реНрдЯрдВ рдЧреБрдгрд┐рдЧрдгрдореМрд▓рд┐рдордгреЗрдГ рд╢рд╢рд┐рдкреНрд░рднреЛрд╕реНрддреБ реереирем рее

If the ascendant and the Moon are aspected by benefics, results will be good. But if they are aspected by malefic planets evil results happen. Thus have been declared the results arising from the Moon.

NOTES: Prithuyasas has rightly pointed out the necessity for considering Lagna and the Moon before judging the results-

рее рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗрдиреНрджреНрд╡реЛрд░реНрд╡рдХреНрддрд╡реНрдпрдВ рд╢реБрднрджреГрд╖реНрдЯреНрдпрд╛ рд╢реЛрднрдирдорддреЛрд╜рдиреНрдпрддреН рее

From sloka 20 onwards the author has given the combinations which indicate success in the pursuit of the object of the query. Sanketa Nidhi also details almost similar combinations. Sloka 9 of Sanketa VII and slokas 21, 22 and 23 of Sanketa VIII refer. They are general statement of facts.

Neelakantha has however dealt with this subject scientifically and appears more convincing. He says that the querist will gain the object of his desire if the

1. lagna lord aspects the lagna and the lord of the house associated with the query aspects the Relevant house.

or

2. Lagan lord aspects the lord of the query or vice versa

In short, Neelakantha establishes a relationship, direct or indirect, between the success in the achievement of the object of

1. Prasna Jnana, Sloka 10.

query and the planetary combinations Slokas 11 and 12 in Miscellanious chapter of the Tajika Neelakanthi refer.

рее рдЗрддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реАрджреИрд╡рдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрд╛ рд╕реБрдмреЛрдзрд┐рдиреА рднрд╛рд╖рд╛ рдЯреАрдХрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рд╢реБрднрд╛рд╜рд╢реБрднрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпреЛ рджреНрд╡рд┐рддреАрдпрдГ рее

Here ends Chapter Il entitled “Good and Bad Results” of Daivajnavallabha.

THIRD

Gains and Losses

рд▓рд╛рднрд╛рд╜рд▓рд╛рднрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ

рд▓рд╛рднрд╛рд╕реНрддрдкрдВрдЪрд╕рд╣рдЬреЗрд╖реБ рд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╛рдГ

рд╕реНрдпреБрд░реНрд▓рд╛рднрдкреНрд░рджрд╛ рджрджрддрд┐ рдиреЗрд╖реНрдЯрдлрд▓рд╛рдирд┐ рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рдГ ред

рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдВ рд╢реБрднрд╛ рджрд╢рдорд╕рдкреНрддрдордЧрд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рджрджреНрдпреБрд░реНрдорд╛-

рдирд╛рд░реНрдерджрд╛ рджреНрд╡рд┐рддрдпрдкрдВрдЪрдорд▓рдЧреНрдирдЧрд╛рд╢реНрдЪ реерез рее

If benefics are placed in the 11th, 7th, 5th and the 3rd houses they cause gain.Malefics placed in these houses do not yield desired result. Benefics placed in the 10th or 7th bestow status and position upon the native. When they are placed in the 2nd, 5th or 1st house they confer respect, honour and wealth upon the native.

NOTES: The tenth house represents honour, respect, status and rank. The seventh is a Kendra and planets therein fully aspect the lagna.

The 10th house is one of status. Being 10th to 10th, the 7th house too can be considered as the house of status. Hence benefics in the 7th and 10th house are conducive to status. The benefics in the ascendant are conducive to name and fame, because like the 10th, the first house too stands for name and fame. The 2nd- and 5th are houses of wealth. Benefics in these houses will naturally enhance wealth.

Prithuyas in Shatpanchashika says the same thing. Sloka 2 in Chapter 4 refers. He says that when benefis occupy the 3rd, 5th, 11th and 7th house they are indicative of gains. Malefics in the same places are not conducive to good results.

1.

Compares рд╖рдЯреНрдкрдВрдЪрд╢рд┐рдХChap. IV, SI. 2-3

Here we need a clear definition of labha or gain. There are two types of gains. The one is the gain of position and rank or name and fame. The other gain is in terms of money or wealth. It may also be added here that the one is not the synonym for the other. The astrologer should be quite clear in his divination about what he means. House 11 stands for income or gains in financial terms. House 2 indicates the personal acquisition or the bank balance. The houses touched here are 10 the and 7 the. The former stands for the Karmasthana of the native indicating name, fame and honour. The 7th house is 10th to the 10th and as such may be taken to represent the same port-folio as the 10th house. The eleventh house to the 11th is 9th house and second to the second is the third house. They may also be clubbed together standing for income and personal acquisitions. There should be no ambiguity in the language. Unless the houses concerning economic or material gains are involved the material gains should not be foretold.

рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░рдВ рд╕рдкреНрддрджрд╢рджреНрд╡рд┐рд╖рд╖реНрдард╕рд╣рдЬрд╛рдпрд╕реНрдерд╛рдирд╕рдВрд╕реНрдердВ рд╢реБрднрдГ

рдкрд╢реНрдпреЗрджреНрд╡реИ рдкреНрд░рдорджрд╛рдХреГрддрдВ рд╢реБрднрдлрд▓рдВ рд▓рд╛рднрд╛рджрд┐рдХрдВ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреНрддрджрд╛ ред

рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╛рд╖реНрдЯрдЬрд┐рдирд╡рд╛рддреНрдордЬреЗрд╖реБ рдЪ рднрдпрдВ рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╛рд░реНрдердирд╛рд╢реЛрд╜рд╢реБ-

рдореИрд░реЗрддреЗрд╖реНрд╡реЗрд╡ рдЧрддрд╛рдГ рд╢реБрднрд╛рд╕реНрддреБ рд╢реБрднрджрд╛ рдорд╛рдирд╛рд░реНрде рд╕рдореНрдкрддреНрддрдпреЗ реереи рее

If the Moon is placed in the 7th, 10th, 2nd, 6th, 3rd or 11th places and is aspected by benefics, the person will get good results through a lady or he will have gains through the help of a woman. But if the Moon is placed in the 1st, 3rd, 5th, 8th or 9th houses aspected by evil planets, he will cause fear. There will be destruction or failure in undertakings and expenditure of wealth. If benefics are situated in these houses, they will confer status, wealth, property and other good results upon the native.

NOTES: The Moon, being a feminine planet causes gains etc. through ladies while placed in the auspicious places mentioned above. Care must be taken to ensure that the Moon is not afflicatedin these places by being debilitated etc.

Prithuyasas is of the opinion that only malefics in 1, 3, 5, 8 and

9 cause only good results. It is possible that the author is refering to weak Moon and therefore, a malefic in these places.

There would appear some difficulty about the position of Moon in Kendra and Trikonasthana or the quadrants and trines. Prithuyasas and Varahamihira both assert that benefics in Kendras and Trikonas are a welcome augury. Sloka 1 of Chapter 4 of Shatpanchashika says that when benefics occupy the Kendras and Trikonas or when the Malefics are in places other than the Kendras and the 8th house it should be predicted that the persons concerned will realise their cherished ambitions in full. Moon is considered to be both a benefic and a malefic according to its position of waning and waxing. These sages, it appears, have taken him to be malefic only. Prithuyasas specifically says in sloka 3 of chapter 4 thatрд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗрд╢рд╢реА рди рд╢реБрднрджрд╛ Similarly Varahamihir says that Moon in lagna causes fear.

рддреНрд░рд┐рдХреЛрдгрдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рд▓рдпрдЧрд╛рдГ рд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╛рд╕реНрддрдерд╛рд╜рд╢реБрднрд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рддреНрд░реНрдпрд░рд┐рд▓рд╛рднрдЧрд╛ рдпрджрд┐ ред

рднрд╡рдиреНрддрд┐ рд▓рд╛рднрд╛рдп рддрджрд╛рд╜рд╜рд╢реБ рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрддрд╛рдВ рд╡рд┐рдкрд░реНрдпрдпрд╕реНрдерд╛рд╕реНрддреБ рди рд▓рд╛рднрджрд╛ рдЕрдореА реерей рее

If Benefics are placed in triangular houses and quadrants and malefics in 3, 6, and 11th houses, the querist will have gains very quickly. If they are situated otherwise (in the opposite manner) they do not produce any gain.

NOTE : рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╛рддреНрдкрдВрдЪрдорднрд╛рд╕реНрдп рдХреЛрдгрд╕рдВрдЬреНрдЮрд╛ рд╡рд┐рдзреАрдпрддреЗ ред 5th and 9th houses from the ascendant are termed Kona (triangular) houses. Some include the lagna also. 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th houses are termed Kendra houses. Bhattotpala has stated that if benefics are in Kona houses and Malefics are in Kendra houses, the desired objects are surely accomplished.

рдкрдВрдЪрдордирд╡рдореЛрдкрдЧрддреИрд░реНрдмреБрдзрдЧреБрд░реБрд╢реБрдХреНрд░рд░реНрдпрдпреЗрдкреНрд╕рд┐рддрд╛рд╡рд╛рдкреНрддрд┐рдГред рд╖рдЯреНрддреНрд░рд┐рдХреНрд▓рд╛рднреЛрдкрдЧрддреИрдГ

рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрд┐рд╕реБрддрд╕реВрд░реНрдпрдЬреИрд╕реНрддрджреНрд╡рддреН ред рдЪрд┐рдиреНрджреНрд░рд╢реНрдЪрддреБрд░реНрдереЗ рдпрджрд┐ рд╕рдкреНрддрдореЗ рд╢реБрднреЛ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирдЧреЛ рд╡рд╛

рджрд╢рдореЗ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдиреН рее

1.

Compare,рд╖рдЯреНрдкрдВрдЪрд╢рд┐рдХ Chapter V, Sloka 4.

рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди, Sloka 82.

рд╕рджреНрдпреЛрд╜рд░реНрдерд▓рд╛рднреЛрдордиреБрдЬрд╕реНрдп рд╡рд╛рдЪреНрдпрд╕реНрддрджреЗрддрд┐ рд╕рддреНрдпреЛ рдмрд▓рд┐рд░реЗрд╡рдорд╛рд╣ рее рек рее

Satyacharya and Acharya Bali state that if the Moon is placed in the 4th or 7th house and the Sun in placed in the ascendant or the 10th house, the person has monetary gains immediately.

рд╡реГрд╖рд╣рдпреНрд░реНрдпрд╛рд▓рд┐рдШрдЯреИрдГ рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд┐ рд╡реЗрджрдиреНрди рдЪрд░рд░рд╛рд╢реМ ред

рджреНрд╡рд┐рддрдиреМ рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЛрдкрдЧрддреЗ рдЪрд░рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░реЛрдХреНрддрдВ рдлрд▓рдВ рджрд▓рддрдГ рее рел рее

If the ascendant of query falls in the signs Taurus, Leo, Scorpio or Aquarius the person gains some position (status) or post. If it falls in a movable sign, this does not happen. If the ascendant falls in a dual sign, both results happen.

NOTES: This is the opinion of Prithuyasas and Bhattotpala also. Acharya Siddha Narayana Dasa, however, is of the opinion that the desired object is obtained with difficulty after some time.

“рдЕрднреАрд╖реНрдЯрд╡рд╕реНрддреБ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╢реНрдЪрд┐рд░реЗрдг рдЧрдордирд╛рдЧрдо рдмрдиреНрдзрдореЛрдХреНрд╖рд╛ ред "

реердЗрддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реА рджреИрд╡рдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдп рддреГрддреАрдпрдГрее

Here ends Chapter III entitled “Gains and Losses”.

1. рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╡реИрд╖реНрдгрд╡, Ch. I. Sloka 45.

FOURTH

Travels (Coming and Going) in General

рд╕рд╛рдорд╛рдиреНрдп рдЧрдорд╛рдЧрдорд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ

рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░реЗ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рди рдЧрдорд╛рдЧрдореМ рд╕реНрддрд╕реНрд╡рд░реЗ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рддреБ рд╡рд┐рдирд┐рд╢реНрдЪрд┐рддреМ рддреМ ред

рдорд┐рд╢реНрд░рдВ рдлрд▓рдВ рд╕реНрдерд╛рд╡рд┐рддрдиреМ рддрджрд░реНрдзрдВрджреНрд╡рдпреЗ рдЪрд░рд╕реНрдерд╛рд╡рд░рд╡рддреНрддрджреВрд╣реНрдпрдореН реерезрее

If the ascendant of query falls in a fixed sign, there is no coming and going (i.e., no travels). If it falls in a movable sign, travel (coming and going) definitely occurs. If the ascendant falls in a dual sign, the first and second half of the dual sign produce the results similar to movable and fixed signs.

NOTES: Mesha, Karka, Tula and Makara are movable signs. Vrishabha, Simha, Vrischika and Kumbha are fixed signs. Mithuna, Kanya, Dhanus and Meena aretermed dual signs. If the query relates to travel or return of a person it will take place if the ascendant falls in a Chara (Movable sign). If the lagna falls in the first half of a dual sign, travel etc. will materialise but it will not if the ascendant etc. falls in the second half of the dual sign.

рд╕реВрд░рд╕реМрд░рд┐рдЧреБрд░реБрд╕реМрдореНрдпрд╕рд┐рддрд╛рдирд╛рдореЗрдХрдХреЛрдкрд┐ рдЪрд░рд▓рдЧреНрдирдЧрддрд╢реНрдЪреЗрддреН ред

рдЖрд╢реБ рддрд░реНрд╣рд┐ рдЧрдордирдВ рд╕реНрдкреГрд╣рдгреАрдпрдВ рд╡рдХреНрд░рддрд╛рдореБрдкрдЧрддрд╕реНрддреБ рди рд╣реАрддрд┐ рее реирее

Even if one among the planets Sun, Saturn, Mercury and Venus be placed in the ascendant identical with a Chara (movable sign) travel takes place early. But if this planet is retrograde there will be no travel.

NOTES: As the Sun is never retrograde, the condition of direct motion applies only to the remaining three planets. Prithuyasas has also given this condition in Shatpanchasika.

1.Compare-(1)рд╖рдЯреНрдкрдВрдЪрд╢рд┐рдХрд╛ Chapter II, Slokas 10 and 8.

(2)рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдиSloka 15 to 16.

(3)рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирд╢рд┐рд░реЛрдордгрд┐ Chapter 1, Sloka 25.

рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╡рд░реНрддреА рдЧреБрд░реБрдмреБрдзрд╕рд┐рддрднрд╛рд╕реНрдХрд░реЗрд╖реБ рдпрджреНрдпреЗрдХрдГ ред

рдЧрдВрддреБрдГ рдкрдереЛ рдирд┐рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐рдВ рдЬрдирдпрддрд┐ рдирд┐рдГрд╕рдВрд╢рдпрдВ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдиреЗ рее рей рее

If the ascendant falls in a fixed sign with one among Jupiter, Mercury, Venus or Sun is placed therein, the traveller breaks his journey and returns without any doubt.

рд░рд╡рд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╛ рдЧреБрд░реБрд░реНрд╡рд╛ рдмреБрдзреЛ рд╡рд╛ рд╕рд┐рддреЛ рд╡рд╛ рднрд╡реЗрджрд╛рд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрдГ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдХрд╛рд▓реЗ ред

рдЧрддрд┐рдГ рдкреНрд░рдЪреНрдЫрддрдГ рд╢реАрдШреНрд░рдореЗрд╡рд╛рднрд┐рдзреЗрдпрд╛ рдирд┐рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐рдВ рдкрдереЛрд╜рдореАрдорд┐рд░рдиреНрддреНрдпрд╛рд▓рдпрд╕реНрдпреИрдГ реерек рее

If at the time of query, one of the planets Sun, Jupiter, Mercury or Venus be placed in the eleventh house, the person will have to go out on a journey very early. But if one of these planets be placed in the 12th house, he breaks his journey and returns-Thus one ought to tell.

It seems that the Sun, Mercury, Venus and Jupiter are planets intimately linked to travels. Their location in the house of gains ( 11th) means the gain of travels and their location in 12th a negation of travel.

рд░рд╛рдВрдЧрд┐рд░рд╕реЛрдГ рдкрд░рдпреЗрджреЗрдХреЛрдкрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рдВ рд╕рдореБрджреНрдпрдиреНрддрдореН ред

рдкреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯрд╜рд╜рдЧрдордирдВ рдкреНрд░рдЪреНрдЫреЗрддреНрддрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдЧрдордирдВ рди рд╡рдХреНрддрд╡реНрдпрдореН реерел рее

If the ascendant falls in a fixed sign and even if one of Saturn or Jupiter aspects the same and if the query relates to the return of a person who has gone to distant lands, the reply should be that there, is no return.

рд╖рд╖реНрдарддреНрд░рд┐рдХреЛрдгрд╕рдВрд╕реНрде рдкрд╛рдкреИрд╢реНрдЪ рдкрд╛рдкрд╕рдВрджреГрд╖реНрдЯреИрдГ ред

рдЧрдордирд╛рдЧрдордирдВ рди рд╡рд╛рдЪреНрдпрдВ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдЪреЗрдЪреНрдЪрд░реЗ рддреБ рд╡рд┐рдкрд░реАрддрдореН реерем рее

If the ascendants fall in a fixed sign and there is aspect of malefic planets on the malefics placed in 5, 6, and 9th houses travel is not to be predicted. But if the ascendant falls in a movable sign, travel will take place definitely.

рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░рддреЛрд╜рде рдпрджрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирддреЛ рджреНрд╡рд╛рджрд╢рджреНрд╡рд┐рддрдпрд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рдЧрд╛рдорд┐рдирдГ ред

рд╢реБрдХреНрд░рд╡рд╛рдХреНрдпрддрд┐рд╢рд╢рд╛рдВрдХрдирдиреНрджрдирд╛рдГ рдХрд╛ рдЧрдорд╜рд╜рдЧрдордХрдерд╛рд╜рд╕реНрддрд┐ рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрддрдГ рее рен рее

If Venus, Jupiter or Mercury is placed in the 2nd or 12th sign from Lagna or Chandra lagna what is there to be told about travel, to the querist.

NOTES: That is, there is nothing to be told. In other words travel will not take place. Nor will the person in exile come back.

As already mentioned in Sloka No. 4, Sun is one of the planets causing travels. But there is no mention of the Sun in this sloka. It appears, that the main cause for travel is nature of planets as malefics or benefics. When benefic planets surround the lagna by occupying the 2nd and the 12th house, they naturally influence the lagna and thereby work as shubha factors against giving travels.

Here the sage has told the relationship of journey with the nature of rasi rising in the east at the time of the query that is the lagna. Daivajna Neelkantha in this respect has given more importance to the position of the lord of ascendant and his Ithasaala with other planets. He says that there will be a journey-

(a) if the lagnesha is in Kendra and there is ithasaala with the 9th lord; or

(b) ninth lord occupies the lagna and is in ithasaala with, the legna lord; or

(c) the lagna lord is in the Kendra and is in ithasaala with the planet in the 3rd house and there is no malefic.

Badarayana tells us about the return of the native that it depends upon the planets occupying hourses 2 and 3. Varahamihira also supports the view of Badarayana: when he says

рд▓рдЧреНрдирддрдГ рд╕рд╣рдЬрдкреБрддреНрд░рд╡рд┐рддреНрддрдЧ рджреВрд░рдЧрд╛рдЧрдордирд╢рдВрд╕рд┐рдиреЛ рдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╛рдГ ред

рдирд╖реНрдЯрд▓рдореНрднрдирдХрд░рд╛рдГ рд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╛рдГ рд╢реАрдШреНрд░рдорд╛рдЧрдордХрд░реМ рддреБ рдордиреНрддреНрд░рд┐рдгреМ рее

(If there is a planet in houses 2, 3, 5 the native returns and if Jupiter and Venus in these houses the native returns early).

1. Compare рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди, Sloka 20.

Daivajna Rama Dayalu in Sanketa 8 sloka 34 says that if there is a question whether there will be any journey and if so when, the answer would be that there would be an early journey if the Prasna lagna falls in a movable sign owned by a benefic planet. If the ascendant falls in a fixed sign aspected by Moon there shall be a journey. The ascendant falling in a dual sign indicates that there will be a journey and return.

рдмрд▓реЗрди рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЛрддреНрддрдорддрд╛рдореБрдкрд╛рдЧрддреЛ рдЧреНрд░рд╣реЛ рдЧреГрд╣реЗ рдпрд╛рд╡рддрд┐ рд▓рдЧреНрдирддреЛ рднрд╡реЗрддреН ред

рдкреНрд░рд╡рд╛рд╕рддрд╕реНрддрддреНрд╕рдорд╕рдВрдЦреНрдпрдорд╛рд╕рддреЛ рд╡рд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрдирдВ рдЧрдиреНрддреБрд░рд╕рдВрд╢рдпрдВ рд╡рджреЗрддреН рее рео рее

Time of return: Count the number of the signs in which the strongest planet is placed away from the lagna. The person in exile will return in so many months as indicated by this number. There is no doubt regarding this.

If the said planet is in the navamsha of a movable sign the number of months revealed is as stated. If it is in the navamsha of a fixed sign the time involved will be double and if it is in navamsha of a dual sign it will be three times of it.

рдЪрд░рд╛рдВрд╢рдХрд╕реНрдереЛ рдХрд┐рд▓ рдХрд╛рддреНрдо рдПрд╡рдВ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рд╛рдВрд╢рдХреЗ рддрджреНрд╡рд┐рдЧреБрдгрд╕реНрддреБ рд╡рд╛рдЪреНрдпрдГ ред

рджреНрд╡рд┐рджреЗрд╣рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╛рдВрд╢рдЧрддреЗ рдЧреНрд░рд╣реЗ рд╡рд┐рдЪрд┐рдиреНрддрд┐рддрд╕реНрддрддреНрд░рд┐рдЧреБрдгреЛ рд╡рд┐рдзреЗрдпрдГ рее реп рее

If the strongest planet is placed in a movable navamsha the time period is to be taken as indicated. But if it be in fixed Navamsha, the time period is to be doubled. And if the strongest planet be in a dual navamsha the time period is to be trebled.

NOTES: Suppose the strongest planet is placed in the 4th sign from lagna. If it be in a chara navamsha the period is to be taken as 4 months. If it be in a fixed navamsha, it is to be taken as 8 months. If it be in a dual navamsha the period is to be taken as 3 x 4 = 12 months. But this rule will not apply where the period of return is expected to

1. Compare (i)рд╖рдЯреН рдкрдВрдЪрд╛рд╢рд┐рдХChapter II, Slokas 14 & 15.
(ii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирддрдиреНрддреНрд░Mise, Slokas 22 & 23.
(iii) рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирдЪрдгреНрдбреЗрд╢реНрд╡рд░ Chapter 6, Sloka 13.

be more than three years. So, it can be used only when the person is

expected to return shortly.

рдпрд╛рддреБрдГ рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрд╛рдЬреНрдЮрд▓рдЧреНрдирддрдГ рд╕рдкреНрддрдорд╕реНрдп рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдореА рдпрд╛рдпрд╛рджреНрдпрд╛рд╡рдд рд╡рдХреНрд░рднрд╛рд╡рдореН ред

рдХрд╛рд▓реЗрдиреИрддрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╕реНрддрд╛рд╡рддреЗ рдкреНрд░рд╛рд╣реБрд╕реНрддреНрд╡реЗрддреЗ рдкреНрд░рд╢реНрдирддрддреНрддреНрд╡рдкреНрд░рд╡реАрдгрд╛рдГ рее резреж рее

Scholars, well versed in Horary Astrology declare that at the time when the lord of the 7th house from the ascendant of query becomes retrograde, the person in exile, returns.

NOTES: Acharya Prithuyasas vide (рд╖рдЯреН рдкрдВрдЪрд╛рд╢рд┐рдХ genres Chapter II, Sloka 16) has recommended the time of retrogression of the lord of the 7th house of the ascendant of travel of the traveller. The rule is not without defect as if the ascendant falls in Capricorn or Aquarius lord of the 7th house will be the Sun or the Moon which will never become retrograde. Hence it is obvious that the rule applies only to ascendant to other than Capricorn and Aquarius. The rule is quite cogent as the 7th house is representative of the “way.” And then it would appear that the traveller will never return. Hence the rule requires further investigation.

Additional note

The chapter deals with travels and journey. It would be useful for the lay readers if they know what the various houses of the horary chart stands for.Neelakantha in this respect says that the ascendant stands for the experience of phlysical pleasure and pain or comforts and discomforts on the way. The fourth house indicates the place where the person has gone.

Gaimini in his Gnana Pradeepika has given more detailed an account of the houses. He says that:

(a) lagna stands for health and longevity of the person;

(b) 2nd house for financial gains

(c) 3rd house for persons following or assisting

(d) 4th for return to residence

(e) 5th & 6th for experiences in the journey

(f) 7th house for the place where he has gone
(g) 8th house for troubles in the journey
(h) 9th house for incidents and accidents
(i) 10th house for residence away from home
(j) 11th house for gains and 12th for losses.

рее рдЗрддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реА рджреИрд╡рдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ рдЪрддреБрд░реНрдердГрее

Here ends Chapter IV entitled “Travels in general” of the work

Dalvajnavallabha.

FIFTH

The Invasion and Retreat of Enemies

рд╢рддреНрд░реБрдЧрдорд╛рдЧрдорд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ

рдкрд╛рдкреИ рд░рд┐рдкреБрд╕реНрдереИрд░реНрдпрджрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рд╕реБрддрд╕реНрдпреИрд░реНрдирд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрддреЗ рд╡рд░реНрддреНрдордд рдПрд╡ рд╢рддреНрд░реБрдГ ред

рдЪрддреБрд░реНрдердЧреИрд░рдиреНрддрд┐рдХрд╕рдВрдЧрддреЛрд╜рдкрд┐ рдкрд░рд╛рдЩреНрдореБрдЦреЛ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрддрд┐ рднрдЧреНрдирд╕реИрдиреНрдпрдГрее резрее

If the 5th or 6th house is occupied by malefics the enemy retreats on the way. When malefics are placed in the IV house, the enemy-even though he might have approached very near will have his forces defeated and destroyed and thereafter returns disinterested.

NOTES: If the 4th house is occupied by a malefic, the enemy even when he has come close, retreats after getting his forces destroyed.

It would be relevant here, as in any other case of judging the charts and declaring the results, to know what the various houses stand for in respect of the query. The chapter is regarding the invasion of the enemy and the ultimate results thereof. Shatpanchashika throws some light on the subject. The six houses commencing from the 3rd house of the Prasna lagna stand for the citizens or the town attacked. The other six houses relate to the invaders. The town attacked here may also mean the kingdom as a whole. The benefic or malefic influences on the house 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th, 7th and 8th would therefore indicate the position of the party attacked and those on houses 9th to 2nd about the position of Invaders. Those who go to attack are called the Yayee or the goers and those who are attacked are called the Nagar or the citizens. Results, good or bad, to these houses would reveal the good or bad of the party concerned. Sloka 2 Chapter III give this idea.

рдЪрддреБрд░реНрдердЧреИрд░рд▓рд┐рдореАрдирдХрд░реНрдХрдЯреИрдГ рдкрд░рд╛рдЬрдпреЛ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рд╢реБрдиреИрд░реНрд╡рд┐рд▓реЛрдХрдирд╛рддреН ред
рдЪрддреБрд╖реНрдкрджреИрдГ рдкреБрдирд░рд┐рд╣ рддреБрд░реНрдпрд╡рд░реНрддрд┐рднрд┐рдГ рдкрд▓рд╛рдпрддреЗ рдирд┐рдпрддрдорд░рд╛рддрд┐рд░рд╛рдЧрддрдГ рее реирее

If the fourth house falls in the signs Scorpio, Pisces or Cancer and is aspected by benefic planets the enemy is defeated. If there be a quadruped sign on the fourth house, the enemy who has come with the intention of conquering definitely runs away.

NOTES: Aries, Taurus and Leo which are represented by quadrupeds are called the quadruped signs.

Sanketa Nidhi also says the same thing. Sloka 52 of Sanket VIII refers. If it is a question of victory or defeat and if the ascendant happens to be Aries, Taurus, Leo, Virgo, Sagittarius, Capricorn, Scorpio or Aquarius success may be predicted. This is more so when a strong benefic occupies or aspects the ascendant.

It appears from the various slokas that the houses in such horary charts are fixed irrespective of the querent.

It may also have to be mentioned here that the aspect rather than occupation has its effects on the house concerned. This is apparent from sloka 2 here that fourth house has to be aspected by benefic planets to cause the defeat of the enemy. Fourth house here represents the party attacked. In the Sanketa Nidhi however it says that strong benefic occupies or aspects ascendant. If the benefic occupies the ascendant he will aspect 7th house which relates to the invaded party and as such helpful to him. If the benefic aspects the lagna it helps the invading party. Normally these are not the days of one king attacking the other and as such not much of research can be undertaken.

рдЪрд░реЛрджрдпреЗ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рдпрджрд╛ рд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╕реНрддрджрд╛ рднреГрд╢рдВ рдЬрдирдпрддрд┐ рдпрд╛рдирд┐рдирд╛рдВ рд╢реБрднрдореН ред
рдЪрд░реЛрджрдпреЗ рддреНрд╡рд╢реБрднрд╕рдордиреНрд╡рд┐рддреЗ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░реЛрджрдпреЗ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╡реНрдпрд╡рд╕реНрдердпрд╛ рее рей рее

If the ascendant falls in a movable sign (Chara rasi) and contains a benefic planet, then surely it causes more auspicious results to the kings who attack. If the movable ascendant is combined with a malefic planet surely inauspicious results occur to them. If a

fixed sign rises with benefic planet in it definitely good results are produced.

рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░реЗ рд╢рд╢рд╛рдВрдХреЗ рдЪрд░рд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдирд╡рд╛рдВрд╢рдХреЗ рд╡рд╛рд╜рд╕реНрдпрд░рд┐рдкреБрд╕реНрддрджреИрддрд┐ ред

рдЪрд░реЗ рд╢рд╢рд╛рдВрдХреЗ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдирд╡рд╛рдВрд╢рдХреЗ рддрд╕реНрдп рддреБ рд╡рд╛рдЧрдордГ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН рее рек рее

If the Moon is placed in a fixed sign and the ascendant is on a movable sign, or Navamsha, the enemy surely comes. But if the Moon is in a movable sign and the ascendant falls in a fixed sign or Navamsha, the enemy does not attack.

рд╢реАрддрдЧреМ рджреНрд╡рд┐рддрдиреБрд░рд╛рд╢рд┐рд╕рдВрд╕реНрдерд┐рддреЗ рд▓рдЧреНрдирддрд╛рдореБрдкрдЧрддреЛ рдпрджрд┐ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рдГ ред

рд╢рддреНрд░реБрд░реЗрддреНрдп рд╡рд┐рдирд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрддреЗрд╜рд░рд┐рднреЗ рдЬреНрдЮреЗрдЬреНрдпрд╢реБрдХреНрд░рд╕рд╣рд┐рддреЗ рд╡рд┐рдирд╢реНрдпрддрд┐ рее релрее

If the Moon is in a dual sign, and the ascendant falls in a fixed sign, the enemy comes and then returns. In this combination, if Mercury, Jupiter and Venus are placed in the sixth house, the enemy is destroyed.

NOTES: The principle seems to be that if malefics be placed in the 6th house, the enemy wins. If benefics are placed, he is defeated. Our experience however is that benefics in the 6th do not provoke the enemy for an attack and as such he can be considered as destroyed.

рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░реЗ рдЧреБрд░реБрд╢рдиреИрд╢реНрд╡рд░рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд┐рджреГрд╖реНрдЯреЗ рд╢рддреНрд░реЛрд░реНрди

рд╡рд╛ рдЧрдордирдорд╛рдЧрдордирдВ рди рд╡рд╛ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН ред
рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд┐рдкрдВрдЪрд░рд┐рдкреБрдЧрд╛ рд░рд┐рдкреБрд╕рдВрдЧрдорд╛рдп
рддреБрдпреЗрдВ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╛рдГ рдкреБрдирд░рд░рд╛рддрд┐рдирд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрдирд╛рдп рее ремрее

If the ascendant falls in a fixed sign and is aspected by Jupiter and Saturn then either the enemy does not come or he may not go back after attacking. If malefics are placed in 3, 5 and 6 the enemy has to be faced. If they are placed in the 4th house, the enemy surely returns.

NOTES: In Shatpanchashika also we come across the same things. Sloka 10 of chapter II refers.

рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░реЛрджрдпреЗ рдЬреАрд╡рд╢рдиреИрд╢реНрдЪрд░реЗрдХреНрд╖рд┐рддреЗ рдЧрдорд╛рдЧрдореМ рдиреИрд╡ рд╡рджреЗрддреН рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрддрдГ
рддреНрд░рд┐рдкрдВрдЪрд╖рд╖реНрдард╛ рд░рд┐рдкреБрд╕рдВрдЧрдорд╛рдп рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рд╢реНрдЪрддреБрд░реНрдереА рд╡рд┐рдирд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрдирд╛рдп ред

Here it may be relevant to refer to Sanketa Nidhi which says when there would be a declaration of war and when there would be a compromise etc.

рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╢реНрд╡рд░реЗ рджреНрд╡рд┐рддрдиреБрд▓рдЧреНрдирдордереЛ рдкрдереЛрд╜рд░реНрдзрдорд╛рдЧрддреНрдп

рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрддрд┐ рд░рд┐рдкреБрд░реНрджреНрдзрд┐рддрдиреМрдЪ рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░реЗ ред
рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдЪрд░реЗ рд░рд┐рдкреБрд░реБрдкреИрддрд┐ рдмрд▓рджреНрд╡рдпреЗрди
рдкрд╛рдкреЗрдХреНрд╖рдгрд╛рджреНрднрд╡рддрд┐ рддрд╕реНрдп рдкрд░рд╛рдЬрдпреЛрд╜рдкрд┐ рееренрее

If the Moon is placed in a movable sign and the ascendant falls in a dual sign the enemy comes half way and then returns. If the Moon is placed in a dual sign and the ascendant falls in a movable sign, the enemy comes with two armies. But if the ascendant and the Moon are aspected by malefic planets, he is defeated also.

NOTES: Compare Sloka, &, Chapter II of Shatpanchashika. If there be benefic aspect over the ascendant and the Moon, the enemy will win.

рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдХреМ рдпрджрд┐ рд╣рд┐рдореБрд▓реЗ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддреЛ рднрд╡реЗрддрд╛рдорддреНрдпреБрдЧреНрд░рдВрди рд╣рд┐ рдкрд░рдЪрдХреНрд░рдорднреНрдпреБрдкреИрддрд┐ ред
рдЖрдХреНрд░рд╛рдиреНрдд рдЧреБрд░реБрдмреБрдзрднрд╛рд░реНрдЧрд╡реИрд╢реНрдЪрддреБрд░реНрде рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдВ рдЪреЗрддреНрддреНрд╡рд░рд┐рддрдореБрдкреИрддреНрдпрд░рд┐рд╕реНрддрджрд╛рдиреАрдореН рее рео рее

If the Moon and the Sun are situated in the 4th house, the terrible army of the enemy does not come. But if the 4th house is occupied by Jupiter, Mercury and Venus the enemy comes very soon.

NOTES: Sloka 11 of S. P. gives the same rule. This is in full agreement with the rule given by Sloka 1 of this Chapter. Moon with the Sun becomes weak and so the enemy does not come. (рдЪрддреБрд░реНрдердЧреИрдГ рдкрд░рд╛рдЩреНрдореБрдЦреЛ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрддрд┐ рднрдЧреНрдирд╕реИрдиреНрдпрдГ ). Jupiter, Mercury and Venus being benefics, the army comes quickly.

рд╕рд┐рдВрд╣рд╛рдЬрдХреЛрджрдгреНрдбрд╡реГрд╖рд╛ рднрд╡рдиреНрддрд┐ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирдЧрд╛ рд╡рд╛рдкрд┐ рдЪрддреБрд░реНрдердЧрд╛ рд╡рд╛ ред
рдЧреНрд░рд╣реЗрдг рдпреБрдХреНрддрд╛ рдпрджрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рд╡рд┐рдпреБрдХреНрддрд╛ рдзреНрд░реБрд╡рдВ рддрджрд╛ рддрд┐рд╖реНрдарддрд┐ рдиреИрд╡ рд╢рддреНрд░реБрдГ реерепрее

If the ascendant or the fourth house falls in the signs Leo, Aries, Sagittarius and Taurus and if no planet is situated in these places then also enemy will not be able to stay. This is certain.

NOTES: Prithuyasas says рд╢рддреНрд░реБрд░реНрдирд┐рд╡рд░реНрддреНрддрддреЗ i.e, the enemy retreats, to his place. According to the dictum “рдЪрддреБрд╖реНрдкрджреИрдГ рдкреБрдирд░рд┐рд╣рддреБрд░реНрдпрд╡рд░реНрддреНрддрд┐рднрд┐рдГ рдкрд▓рд╛рдпрддреЗ рдирд┐рдпрддрдорд░рд╛рддрд┐рд░рд╛рдЧрддрдГ” sloka 2 of this chapter, the enemy retreats. The additional point is, even if lagna falls in beastial signs, the enemy retreats. [The rreason may be : As these beasts are capable of running, the indication is that the enemy will run away.]

рд░рд╡реМ рдЧреБрд░реМ рд╡рд╛ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рд▓рдЧреНрди рдЧрд╛рдорд┐рдирд┐ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддреЛ рд░рд┐рдкреБрдГ рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рд╢реНрд░рдо рдПрд╡ рдирд┐рд╢реНрдЪрд▓рдГ ред
рд░рд╡реМ рдЧреБрд░реМ рд╡рд╛рде рдЪрд░реЛрджрдпрд╕реНрдерд┐рддреЗ рд╡рджреЗрджрд░рд╛рддреЗрд░рдЪрд┐рд░рд╛рддреНрд╕рдорд╛рдЧрдордореН реерезрежрее

If there be a fixed sign on the ascendant and if it is occupied by the Sun or Jupiter, the enemy is quiet in his own place. But if the same planets are placed in a movable sign in the ascendant, it should be told that the enemy will come soon.

NOTES: This result is due to the influence of the movable and fixed signs which has already

been

discussed.

рд╕реБрд░рд╛рдЪрд╛рд░реНрдпрджреЗрд╡рджреНрд╡рд┐рд╖рдиреНрдордиреНрддреНрд░рд┐рдгреМрджреНрд╡реМрджреНрд╡рд┐рддреАрдпреЗ рддреГрддреАрдпреЗ рдпрдерд╛ рд╡рд╛ рддрдерд╛ рд╡рд╛ ред
рддрджрд╛ рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдкреНрд░рдорд╛рдпрд╛рддреНрдпрд░рд╛рддрд┐рдГ рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рд╕реНрдереИрд░реНрди рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗрд╢рдзрд░реНрдореЗрд╢рдХрд░реНрдореЗрд╢рдореЗрд╢реИрдГ реерезрезрее

If Jupiter and Venus are placed separately or together in the second or the third house, the enemy comes very soon. If the lords of the Ist, 9th and 10th house are placed in fixed signs, the enemy never

comes.

рдпрд╡рд╛рддреНрд╕рдВрдЦреНрдпрдВ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рд░рдЬрдиреАрдирд╛рдердЧреЗрд╣рдВ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╛рдиреНрдиреИрдХреЛрд╜рдкрд┐
рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдиреНрдирд┐рдпрддрдордирдпреЛрд░реНрдордзреНрдпрд╡рд░реНрддреА рдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╢реНрдЪреЗрддреН ред

рддрд╛рд╡рддреНрд╕рдВрдЦреНрдпреИрд░рдкрд┐ рдЧрддрджрд┐рдиреИрдГ рд╢рддреНрд░реБрд░рд╛рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрддреАрддрд┐
рдЬреНрдпреЛрддрд┐рд░реНрд╡рд┐рджреНрдпрд╛рд╡рд┐рдкреБрд▓рдЧрдгрдХрдЧреНрд░рд╛рдордгреАрд░реБрджреНрдЧреГрдгрд╛рддрд┐ реерезреи рее

The time of attack of the enemy: If there be no planet between the ascendant and the Moon, the enemy will attack in as many days as are indicated by the house occupied by the Moon from the Lagna.

NOTES: Bhattotpala, commenting on Sloka 17, Chapter II of S. P. says that if there be an intervening planet between the ascendant and the Moon, the enemy will not come.

It would be useful here to refer to Gaimini’s Gnana Pradeepika where he has identified the house for the invaders and for those who are attacked. The houses 4 to 9 of the horary chart tell us about the enemy or the invader. The houses 10 to 3 indicate the position of the other party. The position of malefics and benefics in the group and their strength or weaknesses etc. will help us in determining the final results. This is almost confirmed by the Shatpanchasika. It says that the six houses commencing from the 3rd relate to the citizens or the town attacked. The benefic planets in these houses help the chief of the town attacked.

Daivajna Neelakantha has said when there will be peace between the invading and the invaded kings, when there will be victory or defeat etc.

рее рдЗрддрд┐ рд╢реНрд░реА рджреИрд╡рдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдп рдкрдВрдЪрдордГ рее

Here ends Chapter V entitled “The Invasion and Retreat of Enemies” of Daivajnavallabha.

SIXTH

Queries about one who is Abroad
рдкреНрд░рд╡рд╛рд╕рдЪрд┐рдиреНрддрд╛рдзреНрдпрд╛рдпрдГ

рд▓рдЧреНрдирддрдГ рд╕рд╣рдЬрдкреБрддреНрд░рд╡рд┐рддреНрддрдЧрд╛ рджреВрд░рдЧрд╛рдЧрдордирд╢рдВрд╕рд┐рдиреЛ рдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╛рдГ ред
рдирд╖реНрдЯрд▓рдореНрднрдирдХрд░рд╛рдГ рд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣рд╛рдГ рд╢реАрдШреНрд░рдорд╛рдЧрдордХрд░реМрддреБ рдордиреНрддреНрд░рд┐рдгреМрее рез рее

If all the planets are situated in 3rd, 5th and 2nd houses the person who has gone abroad surely returns. Benefics in these places cause the retrieval of lost objects. If Jupiter or Venus is placed there the person returns quickly.

NOTES : Badarayana says in this context:

рд▓рдЧреНрдирд╛рджреН рджреНрд╡рд┐рддреАрдп рднрд╡рдирдВ рддреГрддреАрдпрдВ рд╡рд╛ рдЧреНрд░рд╣реЗрдг рд╕рдВрдпреБрдХреНрддрдореН
рджреВрд░рдЧрддрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдЧрдорди рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐рдордерд╡рд╛ рд╡рд┐рдирд┐рд░реНрджрд┐рд╢рддрд┐ ред

The saged says that the houses 2, 3, 5 indicate that the person gone out is planning to come back. If there are planets occupying these houses the person shall come back. He does not differentiate between the benefic and malefic planets here.

Returning home means the second house. Second to second house is the 3rd house. The 3rd house stands for journey. There should be some journey involved in coming back. The third to 3rd house is the 5th house. Thus for the return of the person on the basis of Bhavat Bhawam the three houses, namely 2nd, 3rd and 5th should be judged.

рдмреГрд╣рд╕реНрдкрддреМ рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдЧрддреЗ рддреБ рдХрд╢реНрдЪрди рдЧреНрд░рд╣реЛ рднрд╡реЗрддреН рд╖рд╖реНрдардЧрддреЛрд╜рде рд╕рдкреНрддрдордГ ред
рднрд╡реЗрддреНрддрджрд╛ рдкреНрд░реЛрд╖рд┐рдд рдкреБрд░реБрд╖рд╛рдЧрдорд╕реНрддреНрд░рд┐рдХреЛрдгрдЧреЗ рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╕реБрддреЗ рд╕рд┐рддреЗрд╜рдкрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рее реи рее

If Jupiter is situated in a quadrant and there is a planet in the 6th or 7th then the person who has gone abroad returns. Similarly, if

Mercury or Venus is placed in the 5th or 9th houses the person returns.

NOTES: Vide Sloka of Chapter V of S. P. also. It is a general principle that, if the quadrants and trines are occupied by benefic auspicious results happen.

рдЕрд╖реНрдЯрдореЗ рд╢рд╢рд┐рдирд┐ рдкрд╛рдкрд╡рд░реНрдЬрд┐рддреЗ рдХрдВрдЯрдХреЗ рд╕реБрдЦрдореБрдкреИрддрд┐ рдЪрд╛рдзреНрд╡рдЧрдГ ред
рдХрдВрдЯрдХрд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╢реБрднрдЧреНрд░рд╣реИрдГ рд╢реБрднрдВ рд╕реНрд╡рдВ рдирд┐рд╡рд╛рд╕рдордпрдореЗрддрд┐ рд▓рд╛рднрд╡рд╛рдиреН реерей рее

If the Moon is placed in the 8th house, and there is no malefic in the angles the person who has gone abroad returns happily. If there is a benefic planet in the angles, he returns with gains.

NOTES: The quadrants are to be free from malefic influence. This is a general principle for good results.

рдкреГрд╖реНрдареЗ рд▓рдЧреНрдиреЗ рдкрд╛рдкрджреГрд╖реНрдЯреЗ рд╡рдзреЛ рд╡рд╛ рдмрдиреНрдзреЛ рд╡рд╛ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреНрд╕реМрдореНрдпрджреГрд╖реНрдЯреЗ рддреБ рди рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН ред
рдкрд╛рдкреЗ рд╖рд╖реНрдареЗ рдХреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдЧреЗ рд╡рд╛ рддреГрддреАрдпреЗ рдирд╖реНрдЯреЛ рднреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯрд╛ рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирддрдГ рдкреНрд░рдЪреНрдпреБрддреЛ рд╡рд╛ реерек рее

If a pristhodaya sign happens to be the ascendant and the same is aspected by a malefic, the person who has gone abroad is dead or he is in jail. If the ascendant is aspected by a benefic planet, the bad results do not happen. If a malefic is placed in the 6th, Kendra or 3rd house the person is either lost, gone elsewhere or has fallen from his position.

NOTES: Some interpret the results serially i.e., if, under the aboue conditions, an evil planet is placed in the 6th house, he is totally lost i.e. his whereabouts will not be traceable. If, it is situated in the Kendra, he has gone somewhere else from the place where he had already gone. If the planet is placed in the 3rd house, the person has fallen from his status i.e., he might have met with the losses in his business or might have lost his job etc.

рдпрдерд╛ рддрдерд╛ рдпрджрд┐ рднрд╡рддрдГ рдХрдердВрдЪрди рджреНрд╡рдпреЗ рдЧрдпреЗ рд╕реБрд░рдЧреБрд░реБрджреИрддреНрдпрдордиреНрддреНрд░рд┐рдгреМред
рдкреНрд░рд╡рд╛рд╕рд┐рдирд╛ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рддрджрд╛

рд╜рд╜

рдЧрдореЛ рдиреГрдгрд╛рдВ рддреБрд░реАрдпрдЧреМрдирд┐рдпрддрдЧреГрд╣ рдкреНрд░рд╡реЗрд╢рджреМ

рее релрее

If Jupiter and Venus be placed in the 2nd and 3rd houses in any manner, the person gone abroad, will surely return. If they be

placed in the 4th house, the person gone abroad definitely enters his house (returns).

NOTES: The 2nd house represents family. Benefics there cause re-union with the family i.e., the person will return. 3rd is 2nd to 2nd house.
